We stayed 2 nights,  but should have checked out after one. Would not recommend, nor go again. There are far better places nearby for better value for money.

msg:I went to Boao on a business trip and booked this resort hotel. It takes about 30 minutes to take a taxi from Boao Airport to the hotel, which costs about 60 yuan. The hotel is very close to Boao Town, and it only takes 5 minutes to get there by taxi for 10 yuan. There are many places to eat in Boao Town.
The front desk clerk Xiaofang was very friendly and took the initiative to help upgrade the 180-degree unbeatable sea view room for free. You can see the sunrise over the sea in the morning. There is a small balcony. You can watch movies in the evening with the sea breeze. Life is very comfortable.
The room is large, and the bathroom has a bathtub and a shower room, which can meet various needs. The only drawback is that the hotel restaurant only provides breakfast.

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Sunshine Family Suite - Sea-View (Affiliated building)
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:7 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted February 20, 2024
msg:I have to praise this hotel here. I didn't expect much when I booked it, but I didn't expect it to give me a big surprise.
First of all, the room is clean and dry, parking is timely, and the service attitude is friendly.
Let me talk about a few amazing details: First of all, the sea view of the sea view suite we booked is really invincible. The Boao sea view at 3 pm is absolutely beautiful.
The second point is that the hotel's smart toilet is very smart. It is not an ordinary smart toilet cover. It has very complete functions. Many five-star hotels are not equipped with such advanced smart toilets, which makes people feel happy.
The third point is that although the hotel's swimming pool is not big, it is clean, comfortable and well maintained, which is very suitable for children to swim.
The fourth point is that although the hotel's children's playground is indoors and the area is not large, it is very playable. There are no fancy money-eating machines, just climbing cars, trampolines, etc., and the children have a lot of fun.
The fifth point is that it is very close to the beach, the waves are very gentle and the sand is fine, which is suitable for children to play.
A suggestion is that the breakfast preparation is not sufficient. In the case of a surge in tourists, I feel that the restaurant is not responsive enough and the dishes are added slowly.
Finally, let's talk about the travel photography. It is very beautiful, mainly because of the blessing of the beautiful scenery. The experience is really great. I will book it next time.

Daoji Hotel seems to be a hotel hidden among green plants. It is only across the road from the sea. Sitting on the balcony, you can not only watch the waves and listen to the sound of the waves, but also watch the sunrise. You can also watch the fireworks on New Year's Eve. How can we not miss this hotel? I will definitely come to Daoji Hotel again next time I have a chance!

If I have to say the shortcomings, I hope this hotel can be loved and recognized by more people. name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Superior Sea View Suite
info:Stayed in July 2021
info:Friends
info:7 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted July 31, 2021
msg:Divide it into two parts
Deduction items:
1. Like some previous reviews, the room cleaning was found to have not been done during check-in, and there were unfinished coke left by the last guest. This hope the hotel must pay attention to it.
2. Facilities need to be upgraded. It’s a big room with few plugs, and you have to unplug the lamp to free up the plug for charging. This doesn’t feel good
3. Too many cabinets are actually useless. The common safes in four-star and five-star hotels do not. After all, there must be some valuables (such as the camera and drone I brought), and I can't bring it with me at any time. I hope to make up for it.
3. This lobby is really not like a four-star hotel lobby. It is not open and a**ospheric. Although it does not affect the accommodation, it will definitely have some impact on new guests.
bonus
1. The location is very good, very close to the beach. The beach is not close, long and wide, and very flat. It is very safe to get to the belly button when it is far away from the sea. Swimming is average, but playing with waves is great. The waves here are relatively large, but not dangerous. It is especially suitable for guests who don’t know how to swim and want to feel in the sea. Observed these few days, there are not many people, but there are shower facilities on the beach, which is really awesome. Not to mention the softness of the sand, the key is that there are no shells that are common on other beaches, and it is perfect to walk up without piercing your feet.
2. The service is still good. The front desk, cleaners and restaurant staff are polite and respect the guests. This is still in line with the four-star standard.
3. Although the hotel is about three kilometers away from Boao Town (a lively place), it is particularly good for taxis. Generally, the order is received within ten seconds, and it is less than ten yuan to go to the town. There is also a small yellow car at Xiaojiekou downstairs, so you can ride it yourself, which is convenient. We can walk back to the hotel from Boao Town along the beach or Binhai Road, and it takes only half an hour. The road is good (only a short distance from the hotel is not so good, but you can borrow the beach park).
4. The restaurant is not expensive (of course it is relative), and it is acceptable to travel out. The breakfast is full of varieties (Chinese, Western, and local). Basically, there are seats when you come.
5. After living for a few days, I feel that the air conditioner works well. However, the toiletries are average, and there is still a gap between the four stars. A deposit is required for check-in (Alipay WeChat can be used), and it will be credited soon after check-out.
If the interior design of this hotel is upgraded to be more modern, I think it is difficult to compare with other hotels in the vicinity.

msg:感謝酒店提供的周到服務和熱情款待，工作人員友善而專業，時刻準備着滿足我的需求。無論是入住期間的問題解答還是關於酒店設施的建議，他們總是樂於幫助並給予細緻的指導。


服務：

酒店的旅拍服務為我的旅行增添了許多特別的回憶。我很喜歡他們的專業攝影師團隊，他們耐心聆聽我的需求並利用自己的技巧和經驗為我拍攝出精美的照片。這些照片成為了我旅行中最寶貴的紀念品，讓我可以隨時回憶起在酒店度過的美好時光。

設施：

酒店擁有兩個泳池也是一個很大的亮點。我可以根據自己的喜好選擇適合自己的泳池。一個泳池的水深為1米，非常適合我這種不擅長游泳但想要放鬆身心的人；而另一個泳池的水深達到1.4米，非常適合喜歡游泳和水上運動的人。這讓我可以根據自己的需要選擇適合自己的泳池，享受水上活動的樂趣。

環境：

酒店位置優越，距離玉帶灘衹需步行短短5分鐘即可抵達。這個便捷的距離為我提供了充分的時間和機會去欣賞海灘的美景，感受大自然的寧靜與宜人。

msg:客觀地講：
第一、酒店位置不錯，陽台能看到大海，視野很好、很漂亮；
第二、設施很一般，體驗很差的是，洗衣機排水管風化了，酒店居然不知道，沒法使用，而且居然沒有配洗衣液，在提出要求後酒店明確表示不能提供，讓自己上**買，不能提供你給洗衣機幹啥，誰旅遊還隨身帶洗衣液？結果酒店安排人把排水管包了，買了洗衣液，洗了衣服後，衣架不夠，讓酒店送一下，就送了半個小時，晾好衣服都晚上十二點多了，真是窩火！
第三、早餐很一般，沒什麼東西可選擇，尤其差的事，炒飯乾的有點扎嘴，也是服了……
總的來説，我們住的副樓，它就不是酒店，它是民宿，整體感覺，對不住這麼好的海景和視野，性價比不高。

posted:Posted January 30, 2023
msg:衹能説這是一家地理位置極佳，但是服務和設施完全不在一個水準的酒店。基本就是90年代那種迎賓館的設計。可能因為靠海的原因，進房間門就是一股黴味，而且怎麼吹也吹不散，半夜睡覺直接被這味道整的睡不着。衞生間的玻璃膠條密封不佳，洗澡水會漏到外面。吹風機基本就像一次性的那種。而且牆上打死的蚊子屍體和血都在，打掃衞生的同事那麼明顯也不去擦掉嗎？電視機很小分辨率很低，而且根本連不上網。如果對衞生條件以及睡眠質量有要求的人不建議選擇。早飯的水準大概三星級的樣子，好在價格便宜，成人88。酒店後門到沙灘大概100米的距離很近。可惜了這麼好的地理位置，如果可以重新裝修好好經營應該是個很好的酒店。再重新裝修前我本人是不會二刷了。
以上完全是本人入住的直觀體驗，不存在任何誇大和捏造。

msg:設施：有游泳池還挺好，臨近海邊也很不錯。
衞生：尚可，房間略有黴味，需要一直開空調換氣，衞生間中規中矩。
環境：泳池和海邊是值得推薦，早上晚上天氣涼爽時散步游泳都是很不錯
服務：前台主管呂娟的工作態度很和藹，辦理入住時很快，還送給小孩子禮物，相當友好親切。住宿期間需要的餐具和紅酒開瓶器也很及時送到。
不足之處：最近酒店在裝修，偶爾會聽到噪音，好在是白天基本不影響休息；中午酒店餐廳不提供午飯，如果早飯吃的晚也還可以接受；洗的襯衣T恤放一晚還是濕漉漉的，如果有除濕機會更好些。

msg:博鰲的酒店服務真的是差！
這還是當地生意最好的一家，還五鑽！攜程怎麼評的！
到酒店行李沒有人拿，保安就那麼看着我們吃力的拖行李，還交按金，什麼年代了，還要交按金，是怕客人偷了他們的馬桶嗎？
健身房破破爛爛，器械沒有一個能用的，這不是忽悠人嗎？連個啞鈴都沒有！
房卡丟了居然要求賠償50塊，現在快捷酒店都不用賠償。
我們的貼身衣物放衞生間打算吃完飯回來清洗，結果被客房服務員給扔了，我們找酒店問詢客房服務員，就説一句沒見到！

最誇張的是，我們都退房退了半天了，結果酒店系統還沒有退出來，導致我們在下一家酒店沒法入住，又打電話回酒店去交涉，靠！
更可笑的是，退房以後還有一個所謂的客服代表打電話來問我入住感受，我跟他説完以後，他居然不好意思的把電話掛了！
永遠不會再住這家酒店！
